Remove(path string) error { return nil }\n\n// WatchUntil watches the specified path for changes and blocks until ctx is canceled.\n// eventHandler() must be non-nil, and pollInterval must be greater than 0.\n// eventHandler() is invoked whenever a change event is observed or pollInterval elapses.\n// errorHandler() is invoked (if non-nil) whenever an error occurs initializing or watching the specified path.\n//\n// If path is a directory, only the directory and immediate children are watched.\n//\n// If path does not exist or cannot be watched, an error is passed to errorHandler() and eventHandler() is called at pollInterval.\n//\n// Multiple observed events may collapse to a single invocation of eventHandler().\n//\n// eventHandler() is invoked immediately after successful initialization of the filesystem watch,\n// in case the path changed concurrent with calling WatchUntil().\nfunc WatchUntil(ctx context.Context, pollInterval time.Duration, path string, eventHandler err != nil {\n    93→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"error while processing inotify event (%+v): %v\", event, err)\n    94→\t\t\t}\n    95→\t\tcase err = <-w.Errors:\n    96→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"error while watching %q: %v\", s.path, err)\n    97→\t\t}\n    98→\t}\n    99→}\n   100→\n   101→func (s *sourceFile) produceWatchEvent(logger klog.Logger, e *fsnotify.Event) error {\n   102→\t// Ignore file start with dots\n   103→\tif strings.HasPrefix(filepath.Base(e.Name), \".\") {\n   104→\t\tlogger.V(4).Info(\"Ignored pod manifest, because it starts with dots\", \"eventName\", e.Name)\n   105→\t\treturn nil\n   106→\t}\n   107→\tvar eventType podEventType\n   108→\tswitch {\n   109→\tcase (e.Op & fsnotify.Create) > 0:\n   110→\t\teventType = podAdd\n   111→\tcase (e.Op & fsnotify.Write) > 0:\n   112→\t\teventType = podModify\n   113→\tcase (e.Op & fsnotify.Chmod) > 0:\n   114→\t\teventType = podModify\n   115→\tcase (e.Op & fsnotify.Remove) > 0:\n   116→\t\teventType = podDelete\n   117→\tcase (e.Op & fsnotify.Rename) > 0:\n   118→\t\teventType = podDelete\n   119→\tdefault:\n   120→\t\t// Ignore rest events\n   121→\t\treturn nil\n   122→\t}\n   123→\n   124→\ts.watchEvents <- &watchEvent{e.Name, eventType}\n   125→\treturn nil\n   126→}\n   127→\n   128→func (s *sourceFile) consumeWatchEvent(logger klog.Logger, e *watchEvent) error {\n   129→\tswitch e.eventType {\n   130→\tcase podAdd, podModify:\n   131→\t\tpod, err := s.extractFromFile(logger, e.fileName)\n   132→\t\tif err != nil {\n   133→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"can't process config file %q: %v\", e.fileName, err)\n   134→\t\t}\n   135→\t\treturn s.store.Add(pod)\n   136→\tcase podDelete:\n   137→\t\tif objKey, keyExist := s.fileKeyMapping[e.fileName]; keyExist {\n   138→\t\t\tpod, podExist, err := s.store.GetByKey(objKey)\n   139→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   140→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   141→\t\t\t}\n   142→\t\t\tif !podExist {\n   143→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"the pod with key %s doesn't exist in cache\", objKey)\n   144→\t\t\t}\n   145→\t\t\tif err = s.store.Delete(pod);
